So, as we honor our veterans, let‚Äôs do so by recognizing those here in Ventura County who live their lives, and have given their lives, in pursuit of a higher ideal. The ideal of community, of purpose, and of selflessness.
I saw it in our own Sheriff Geoff Dean, days from retirement, who lost a friend and who stood strong during this terrible ordeal so that others could find strength through him. And I saw it in all of our first responders, who sacrifice for our community every single day.
I saw it in the actions of Sgt. Ron Helus, who gave his life to save others. I saw it in the young people who carried their friends out of the bar to safety.
On this day each year, we recognize &amp; thank our veterans who embody those qualities &amp; who have served our country w/ such honor &amp; bravery. This year, we also acknowledge others within our community who demonstrate that same selflessness &amp; humility that our vets exemplify daily.
They both symbolize what is so special about the long and proud military tradition here in Ventura County ‚Äî a dedication to the greater good, our shared values, and ceaseless humility and selflessness.
As we remember those who were taken from us this week, I want to mention two of them: Navy veteran Tel Orfanos and Marine veteran Dan Manrique.
As a community, we have weathered significant challenges in the past ‚Äî by coming together and helping where there is need ‚Äî and I know we will do so again.
As our community gathers together this weekend to celebrate and honor our veterans, we must first acknowledge the beautiful lives that were so tragically lost this week at Borderline Bar &amp; Grill.
